***импонировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:импонировать.html>импони́ровать</a> (26948)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">imponieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:импонировать.html>импони́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">imponírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to impress (someone), to make an impression (on someone), to appeal <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ей</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:импонировать.html>импони́ровала</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:храбрость.html>хра́брость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jej <b>imponírovala</b> jevó xrábrostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his courage impressed her</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оппони́ровать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">opponírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">депони́ровать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">deponírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:импозантный.html>импоза́нтный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">impozántnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***импровизировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:импровизировать.html>импровизи́ровать</a> (28662)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">improvisieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:импровизировать.html>импровизи́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">improvizírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to improvise, to extemporize</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сымпровизи́ровать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">symprovizírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:импровизированный.html>импровизи́рованный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">improvizírovannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:импульс.html>и́мпульс</a> (7673)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:импульс.html>и́мпульс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ímpulʹs</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:импульс.html>и́мпульса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:импульс.html>и́мпульсы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:импульс.html>и́мпульсов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:импульсный.html>и́мпульсный</a></b>)

<ol><li>urge, incentive</li>
<li>action potential, spike train</li>

<li>pulse, short electric signal</li></ol>

***имя.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мя</a> (263)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">имѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьmę</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*inˀmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁nómn̥</i>.
</p><p>Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">name</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">noun</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Prussian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Prussian language">Old Prussian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="prg">emmens</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">नामन्</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nāman</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">نام</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nâm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὄνομα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ónoma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">nōmen</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мя</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ímja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мени</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>имена́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>имён</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>name, first name, Christian name, given name (for inanimate things, see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:название.html>назва́ние</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nazvánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мя</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчество.html>о́тчество</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ímja</b> i ótčestvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">first name and patronymic</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мени</a> ста́лина</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zavód ímeni Stálina</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Stalin Automobile Plant</span></div></dd>

***инакомыслие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инакомыслие.html>инакомы́слие</a> (26741)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">инако</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">inako</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьnako</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">otherwise, differently</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">myslʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инакомыслие.html>инакомы́слие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inakomýslije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инакомыслие.html>инакомы́слия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инакомыслие.html>инакомы́слия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инакомыслие.html>инакомы́слий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dissent, dissidence</li>
<li>heterodoxy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>ина́че</a> (579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>ина́че</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>и́наче</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ináče</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ínače</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>differently, in a different way; otherwise
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">по-друго́му</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">po-drugómu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>otherwise, else, or else
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>ина́че</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>и́наче</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>ináče/ínače</b>, kak</i> ― <span class="e-translation">just (like)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>ина́че</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>и́наче</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tak íli <b>ináče/ínače</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">one way or another</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>ина́че</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>и́наче</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говоря́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ináče/ínače</b> govorjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in other words</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***инвалид.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инвалид.html>инвали́д</a> (3812)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">invalide</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инвалид.html>инвали́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">invalíd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инвалид.html>инвали́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инвалид.html>инвали́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инвалид.html>инвали́дов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">инвали́дка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>invalid, disabled person</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инвалидный.html>инвали́дный</a> (17042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инвалид.html>инвали́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">invalíd</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инвалидный.html>инвали́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">invalídnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> disabled, handicapped <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of or for use by a disabled person</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>; disabled person's; invalid's

***инвентарь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инвентарь.html>инвента́рь</a> (16858)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed in the 18th century from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Inventar</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">inventory</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">inventārium</i>; suffix influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́рь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-árʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инвентарь.html>инвента́рь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inventárʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инвентарь.html>инвентаря́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инвентарь.html>инвентари́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инвентарь.html>инвентаре́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>inventory, stock</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инвестировавший.html>инвести́ровавший</a> (24203)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инвестировавший.html>инвести́ровавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">investírovavšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инвестировать.html>инвести́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">investírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
